Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Skylark 048, the Block II Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software for the Skylab-2, Skylab-3, Skylab-4, and Apollo-Soyuz Test Project missions.

They have been created via disassembly of binary dumps of the original core rope memory modules actually flown on Skylab-2, part numbers 2010802-541, 2010802-551, 2010802-561, 2010802-571, 2010802-581, and 2010802-591. Access to these modules was provided by the New Mexico Museum of Space History, who we are much indebted to.

The source code for the Apollo 15, 16, and 17 software, Artemis 072, was used as a starting point. Heavy use was made of TRW 4900.5-244, Programmed Guidance Equations for Skylark Command Module Earth Orbital Program, dated 14 February 1972. This document contains pseudocode of essentially all of Skylark, using original program labels which have been copied for this source reconstruction.

Since only binary dumps (rather than listings) of Skylark are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from the Programmed Guidance Equations or other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

001451,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001452,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001453,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Skylark revision 048.
001454,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC)
001455,000006:                                                                                                  ##              for Skylab-2, Skylab-3, Skylab-4, and ASTP. No original listings of
001456,000007:                                                                                                  ##              this software are available; instead, this file was created via
001457,000008:                                                                                                  ##              disassembly of dumps of the core rope modules actually flown on
001458,000009:                                                                                                  ##              Skylab-2. Access to these modules was provided by the New Mexico
001459,000010:                                                                                                  ##              Museum of Space History.
001460,000011:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001461,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001462,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001463,000014:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2023-09-04 MAS  Created from Artemis 072.
001464,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2024-03-05 MAS  Updated for Skylark 48.
001465,000016: 
001466,000017: 
001467,000018:                                                                                                  ## Erasable definitions have been very heavily changed from Artemis 72.
001468,000019:                                                                                                  ## Unfortunately, since erasables can appear in any order, and a variable
001469,000020:                                                                                                  ## sharing with several others could be equated to any of them, it is
001470,000021:                                                                                                  ## not possible to exactly match what would have been in the original
001471,000022:                                                                                                  ## listing. The order presented here roughly matches that shown in
001472,000023:                                                                                                  ## the Skylark 48 Erasable Memory Map in the MIT Museum's collection.
001473,000024:                                                                                                  ## Flagword definitions have been copied from Skylab/ASTP data cards.
001474,000025: 
001475,000026:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001476,000027: 
001477,000028:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001478,000029:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001479,000030:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001480,000031: 
001481,000032:                                                                                                  #                                        X       EQUALS  START
001482,000033:                                                                                                  #                                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001483,000034:                                                                                                  #                                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001484,000035: 
001485,000036:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001486,000037:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001487,000038:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC,  IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.               )
001488,000039: 
001489,000040: 
001490,000041:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001491,000042:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001492,000043: 
001493,000044:                                                                                                  #                                        X       EQUALS  Y
001494,000045: 
001495,000046: 
001496,000047:                                                                                                  #        = MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001497,000048:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001498,000049: 
001499,000050:                                                                                                  #                                        X       =       Y
001500,000051: 
001501,000052: 
001502,000053:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001503,000054:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001504,000055: 
001505,000056:                                                                                                  #                M REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001506,000057:                                                                                                  #                     B   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001507,000058:                                                                                                  #                         INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001508,000059:                                                                                                  #                     I   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001509,000060:                                                                                                  #                         INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001510,000061:                                                                                                  #                         INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001511,000062: 
001512,000063:                                                                                                  #                SIZE IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001513,000064: 
001514,000065:                                                                                                  #                N INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001515,000066:                                                                                                  #                     PL MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001516,000067:                                                                                                  #                     DSP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001517,000068:                                                                                                  #                     PRM MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001518,000069:                                                                                                  #                         IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001519,000070:                                                                                                  #                         PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001520,000071:                                                                                                  #                     TMP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001521,000072:                                                                                                  #                         IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001522,000073:                                                                                                  #                         IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001523,000074:                                                                                                  #                         PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001524,000075:                                                                                                  #                         CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS
001525,000076:                                                                                                  #                         IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001526,000077:                                                                                                  #                         IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001527,000078:                                                                                                  #                     IN  MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001528,000079:                                                                                                  #                         TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001529,000080:                                                                                                  #                     OUT MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001530,000081:                                                                                                  #                         TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001531,000082: 
001532,000083: 
001533,000084:                                                                                                  #        SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001534,000085: 
001535,000086: ???????                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001536,000087: ???????                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001537,000088: ???????                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001538,000089: ???????                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001539,000090: ???????                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001540,000091: ???????                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001541,000092: ???????                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001542,000093:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001543,000094: 
001544,000095: ???????                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001545,000096: ???????                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001546,000097: ???????                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001547,000098: ???????                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001548,000099: ???????                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001549,000100: ???????                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001550,000101: ???????                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.

001582,000133: ???????  0000053               TVCYAW             EQUALS   CDUTCMD                               #  SPS YAW COMMAND IN TVC MODE.
001583,000134: 
001584,000135: ???????                        CDUSCMD            EQUALS   54                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT COMMAND (WAS OPTXCMD).
001585,000136: ???????  0000054               TVCPITCH           EQUALS   CDUSCMD                               #  SPS PITCH COMMAND IN TVC MODE.
001586,000137:                                                                                                  #  REGISTERS 55-60 ARE COUNTERS WHICH ARE NOT PRESENTLY WIRED, AND SO MAY BE USED WITH CARE
001587,000138: 
001588,000139: 
001589,000140:                                                                                                  #        INTERPRETIVE REGISTERS ADDRESSED RELATIVE TO VAC AREA.
001590,000141: 
001591,000142: ???????                        LVSQUARE           EQUALS   34D                                   #  SQUARE OF VECTOR INPUT TO ABVAL AND UNIT
001592,000143: ???????                        LV                 EQUALS   36D                                   #  LENGTH OF VECTOR INPUT TO UNIT.
001593,000144: ???????                        X1                 EQUALS   38D                                   #  INTERPRETIVE SPECIAL REGISTERS RELATIVE
001594,000145: ???????                        X2                 EQUALS   39D                                   #  TO THE WORK AREA.
001595,000146: ???????                        S1                 EQUALS   40D                                   
001596,000147: ???????                        S2                 EQUALS   41D                                   
001597,000148: ???????                        QPRET              EQUALS   42D

002845,001396:                                                                                                  #          (ITEMP1 THROUGH RUPTREG4)             
002846,001397: 
002847,001398:                                                                                                  #        ANY OF THESE MAY BE USED AS TEMPORARIES DURING INTERRUPT OR WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED. THE ITEMP SERIES
002848,001399:                                                                                                  #  IS USED DURING CALLS TO THE EXECUTIVE AND WAITLIST - THE RUPTREGS ARE NOT.
002849,001400: 
002850,001401:    0061                        ITEMP1             ERASE                                          
002851,001402:    0062     0061               WAITEXIT           EQUALS   ITEMP1                                
002852,001403:    0062     0061               EXECTEM1           EQUALS   ITEMP1

002871,001422:

002874,001425: 
002875,001426:    0070                        RUPTREG1           ERASE                                          
002876,001427:    0071                        RUPTREG2           ERASE                                          
002877,001428:    0072                        RUPTREG3           ERASE                                          
002878,001429:    0073                        RUPTREG4           ERASE                                          
002879,001430:    0074     0073               KEYTEMP1           EQUALS   RUPTREG4

002881,001432:

002890,001441:

002892,001443:                                                                                                  #        EXEC TEMPORARIES WHICH MAY BE USED BETWEEN CCS NEWJOBS. 
002893,001444:                                                                                                  #        (INTB15+ THROUGH RUPTMXM)                                       (32D)
002894,001445: 
002895,001446:    0114                        INTB15+            ERASE                                          #  REFLECTS 15TH BIT OF INDEXABLE ADDRESSES
002896,001447:    0115     0114               DSEXIT             EQUALS   INTB15+                               #  RETURN FOR DSPIN
002897,001448:    0115     0114               EXITEM             EQUALS   INTB15+                               #  RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
002898,001449:    0115                        INTBIT15           ERASE                                          #  SIMILAR TO ABOVE.
002899,001450:    0116     0115               WDRET              EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR DSPWD
002900,001451:    0116     0115               DECRET             EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
002901,001452:    0116     0115               21/22REG           EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  TEMP FOR CHARIN
002902,001453: 
002903,001454:                                                                                                  #  THE REGISTERS BETWEEN ADDRWD AND PRIORITY MUST STAY IN THE FOLLOWING ORDER FOR INTERPRETIVE TRACE.
002904,001455: 
002905,001456:    0116                        ADDRWD             ERASE                                          #  12 BIT INTERPRETIVE OPERAND SUB-ADDRESS.
002906,001457:    0117                        POLISH             ERASE                                          #  HOLDS CADR MADE FROM POLISH ADDRESS.
002907,001458:    0120     0117               UPDATRET           EQUALS   POLISH                                #  RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
002908,001459:    0120     0117               CHAR               EQUALS   POLISH                                #  TEMP FOR CHARIN
002909,001460:    0120     0117               ERCNT              EQUALS   POLISH                                #  COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
002910,001461:    0120     0117               DECOUNT            EQUALS   POLISH                                #  COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
002911,001462: 
002912,001463:    0120                        FIXLOC             ERASE                                          #  WORK AREA ADDRESS.
002913,001464:    0121                        OVFIND             ERASE                                          #  SET NON-ZERO ON OVERFLOW.
002914,001465: 
002915,001466:    0122                        VBUF               ERASE    +5                                    #  TEMPORARY STORAGE USED FOR VECTORS.
002916,001467:    0130     0122               SGNON              EQUALS   VBUF                                  #  TEMP FOR +,- ON
002917,001468:    0130     0122               NOUNTEM            EQUALS   VBUF                                  #  COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
002918,001469:    0130     0122               DISTEM             EQUALS   VBUF                                  #  COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
002919,001470:    0130     0122               DECTEM             EQUALS   VBUF                                  #  COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
002920,001471:

003119,001670:                                                                                                  #  DESIRES TO BYPASS THE CHANNEL REPRESENTATION, HE SHOULD LOAD C31FLWRD   VIA V21 N01 TO THE VALUES SHOWN IN THE

003122,001673:                                                                                                  #     A VALUE      MEANING FOR CHANNEL 31                                     B VALUE      MEANING FOR CHANNEL 33

003125,001676:                                                                                                  #     1            G&N CONTROL FREE                                           1 OR 5       OPTICS MODE CMC
003126,001677:                                                                                                  #     2            G&N CONTROL ATT. HOLD                                      2 OR 6       OPTICS MODE ZERO
